local database = require("Phone/Database")
local triggerMgr = require("Phone/PhoneTriggerManager")
require("Phone/Utils")

local databaseReply = {}

function databaseReply.InitReply()
    -- 这个是总的入口触发器，当玩家选择“问候”时，它会去寻找所有类型为 "reply_问候" 的触发器
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_问候",
        type = "reply",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        bindArgs = "问候",
        event = function(context)
            local cdKey = "reply_greet_cd_" .. context.info.roleId
            if CS.GameCoreHelper.IsCustomCDReady(cdKey) then
                -- 1 天冷却
                CS.GameCoreHelper.SetCustomCD(cdKey, 1)
                -- 随机触发一个 "reply_问候" 类型的事件
                local cachedTriggers = triggerMgr.getCachedTriggersForRole(context.info.roleId, "reply_问候")
                triggerMgr.checkAndExecuteCachedTriggers(context.info.roleId, cachedTriggers, true)

                -- 随机好感
                --[[第6棒：好感度增加内置3天冷却]]
                local cdKey_addFov = "add_fov_" .. cdKey
                if CS.GameCoreHelper.IsCustomCDReady(cdKey_addFov) then
                    context.Delay(1)
                    local fovAdd = math.random(1, 4)
                    --[[第6棒：根据当前好感修正最终值--]]
                    fovAdd = AdjustFinalFov(CS.GameCoreHelper.GetPlayerRole(), context.info.tagRole, fovAdd)
                    ChangeFov(context.info.roleId, fovAdd, true)
                    CS.GameCoreHelper.SetCustomCD(cdKey_addFov, 3)
                    context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, GetFovMessage(context.info.tagRole, fovAdd), "system")
                end
            else
                --[[第6棒：提示冷却时间--]]
                local cdValue = math.floor(CS.GameCoreHelper.GetCustomCD(cdKey))
                context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, string.format("（对方好像暂时没空回复，等%s天后再说吧。）", cdValue), "system")
            end
        end
    })

    --[[
        通用问候对话模板
    ]]

    -- 对话模板1：经典的日常问候
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_问候_通用_1",
        type = "reply_问候",
        weight = 1,
        once = false,
        priority = "normal",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "最近在忙什么？", "主角")
            context.Delay(1.5)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "还能是什么，不是跑商就是和人动手。", context.info.roleId)
            context.Delay(1.5)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "大漠里的日子，不都这样嘛。", context.info.roleId)
        end
    })

    -- 对话模板2：关于路途安全
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_问候_通用_2",
        type = "reply_问候",
        weight = 1,
        once = false,
        priority = "normal",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "在路上吗？注意安全。", "主角")
            context.Delay(1.2)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "刚到营地歇脚，还好没遇上不长眼的沙盗。", context.info.roleId)
            context.Delay(1.5)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "那就好，好好休息。", "主角")
        end
    })

    -- 对话模板3：关于天气和环境
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_问候_通用_3",
        type = "reply_问候",
        weight = 1,
        once = false,
        priority = "normal",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "今天太阳真毒啊，感觉人都快烤干了。", "主角")
            context.Delay(1.5)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "是啊，真想在哪个绿洲里泡上一整天。", context.info.roleId)
        end
    })

    -- 对话模板4：调侃式的问候
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({

        type = "reply_问候",
        weight = 1,
        once = false,
        priority = "normal",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "今天又吃了多少沙子？", "主角")

    })

    -- 对话模板5：关于食物和水

            context.Delay(1)

    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_问候_璨_5",
        type = "reply_问候",
        weight = 5,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        bindRole = "璨",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "我能帮你找回你的记忆吗？", "主角")
            context.Delay(1.5)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "……我感觉，您是我命运中的关键人物。", context.info.roleId)
        end
    })
end

function databaseReply.InitTap()
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_戳一戳",
        type = "reply",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        bindArgs = "戳一戳",
        event = function(context)
            local msg = GetActionMessage(context.info.player, context.info.tagRole, "戳一戳")
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, msg, "system")
            context.Delay(1.5)

            -- 随机触发一个 "reply_戳一戳" 类型的事件
            local cachedTriggers = triggerMgr.getCachedTriggersForRole(context.info.roleId, "reply_戳一戳")
            triggerMgr.checkAndExecuteCachedTriggers(context.info.roleId, cachedTriggers, true)

function databaseReply.InitGift()
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_送礼",
        type = "reply",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        bindArgs = "送礼",
        event = function(context)
            local cdKey = "reply_gift_cd_" .. context.info.roleId
            if CS.GameCoreHelper.IsCustomCDReady(cdKey) then
                -- [[第6棒：在过滤条件中排除不可出售、丢弃的重要道具--]]
                -- local items = ShowItemSelectorDlgAsync("选择礼物", 1, "", context.info.roleId)
                local items = ShowItemSelectorDlgAsync("选择礼物", 1, "[$tagitem:main_type$][<>]4&[$tagitem:tag=NoSellOrDrop$][<>]1&[$tagitem:tag=不可丢弃或出售$][<>]1", context.info.roleId)
                if items == nil or items.Count == 0 then
                    print("玩家取消了送礼")
                    return
                end

                -- 1 天冷却
                --[[第6棒：改为7天]]
                -- CS.GameCoreHelper.SetCustomCD(cdKey, 1)
                CS.GameCoreHelper.SetCustomCD(cdKey, 7)


                local item = items[0]

                context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, GetGiftMessage(item), "主角")

                context.Delay(1)

                context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "（对方接受了你的礼物。）", "system")

                context.Delay(1)
                -- 随机好感
                --[[第6棒：为避免收益过高，改为受到礼物价值影响--]]
                -- local fovAdd = math.random(5, 10)
                local giftValue = item:getSellPrice(true)
                local fovAdd = GetFovByGiftValue(giftValue)
                --[[第6棒：根据当前好感修正最终值--]]
                fovAdd = AdjustFinalFov(CS.GameCoreHelper.GetPlayerRole(), context.info.tagRole, fovAdd)
                ChangeFov(context.info.roleId, fovAdd, true)
                context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, GetFovMessage(context.info.tagRole, fovAdd), "system")

                -- AI尝试装备
                CS.EquipLogic.AITryEquipItem(context.info.tagRole, item, false)

                -- [[第6棒：送礼后移除道具--]]
                CS.GameCoreHelper.RemoveItemsFromPlayerInvByList(items)
            else
                --[[第6棒：提示冷却时间--]]
                local cdValue = math.floor(CS.GameCoreHelper.GetCustomCD(cdKey))
                -- context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, string.format("（对方暂时不想要更多礼物了，等%7。）", "system")
                context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, string.format("（对方暂时不想要更多礼物了，等%s天后再说吧。）", cdValue), "system")
            end
        end
    })
end

--[[第6棒：增加打电话的功能--]]
function databaseReply.InitCall()
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "选项_电话",
        type = "reply",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        bindArgs = "打电话",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMessageRaw(context.info.roleId, "（等待对方接听中……）", "system")

            context.Delay(1)

            local args = CS.GameCoreHelper.CreateEmptyRuntimeArgVal();
            args.CurTagRoleID = context.info.roleId
            CS.GameCoreHelper.CheckGameTrigger("phone_on_call_role", "any", context.info.roleId, args, false)
        end
    })
end

function databaseReply.Init()
    databaseReply.InitReply()
    databaseReply.InitTap()
    databaseReply.InitGift()
    databaseReply.InitCall()
end

return databaseReply
